Instead, your focus is on achieving your goals through strategic manipulation and exploitation of others, which is characteristic of Psychopathy. You're likely to be calculating, detached, and willing to do whatever it takes to get ahead, often without remorse or empathy for those around you. This combination of traits can make you a formidable and intimidating figure, but also potentially isolating and lonely, as you may struggle to form genuine connections with others.
